NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
S. Nithya, a female child born to Thiru R. Selvaraj, on 20th of June 1993, residing at No. 3/280, Raghava Nagar
3rd Main Road, Madipakkam, Chennai-600 091, has been living as a Male after an elaborate Sexual reassignment Surgery
by Dr. Jayaraman, MNAMS, Dip. N.B., Ph.D., FICS Erstwhile Professer of Plastic Surgery, KMC, Chennai-600 010, By this
I, may be treated as a Male and shall henceforth be known as NASEER MOHAMMED. S
Chennai,
